;;;###autoload
(defun anything-mode-map-predefine ()
  "For anything key bindings."
  (interactive)
  (unless (called-interactively-p 'interactive)
    (message "eval-after-load: \"anything\" keymaping.."))
  (define-many-keys anything-map
    ("\C-l"     'forward-char)
    ("\C-j"     'backward-char)
    ("\C-\M-n"  'anything-next-page)
    ("\M-n"     'anything-next-source)
    ("\C-k"     'anything-previous-line)
    ("\C-\M-k"  'anything-previous-page)
    ("\C-b"     'anything-end-of-buffer)
    ("\M-k"     'anything-previous-source)
    ([33554464] 'anything-prev-visible-mark)   ;(kbd S-SPC)
    ("\C-p"     'anything-beginning-of-buffer)
    ("\C-c\C-k" 'anything-kill-marked-buffers)
    ("\C-\M-k" 'anything-kill-marked-buffers)
    ("\C-e"     'anything-execute-persistent-action)
    ("\M-@"     'anything-mark-all)))

* Mon 02 Dec 2013 09:46:33 PM JST
     %a   The abbreviated  weekday name according to  the current
          locale.

     %A   The full weekday name according to the current locale.

     %b   The  abbreviated month  name according  to the  current
          locale.

     %B   The full month name according to the current locale.

     %c   The  preferred date  and  time  representation for  the
          current locale.

     %C   The   century   number    (year/100)   as   a   2-digit
          integer. (SU)

     %d   The day of  the month as a decimal number  (range 01 to
          31).

     %D   Equivalent  to %m/%d/%y.   (Yecch--for Americans  only.
          Americans should note that  in other countries %d/%m/%y
          is  rather common.   This means  that in  international
          context  this format  is  ambiguous and  should not  be
          used.) (SU)

     %e   Like %d, the day of the  month as a decimal number, but
          a leading zero is replaced by a space. (SU)

     %E   Modifier: use alternative format, see below. (SU)

     %F   Equivalent    to    %Y-%m-%d   (the    ISO 8601    date
          format). (C99)

     %G   The ISO 8601  week-based year (see NOTES)  with century
          as a decimal number.  The 4-digit year corresponding to
          the ISO week number (see %V).  This has the same format
          and value  as %Y,  except that if  the ISO  week number
          belongs to the previous or next year, that year is used
          instead. (TZ)

     %g   Like %G, but  without century, that is,  with a 2-digit
          year (00-99). (TZ)

     %h   Equivalent to %b.  (SU)

     %H   The  hour as  a decimal  number using  a 24-hour  clock
          (range 00 to 23).

     %I   The  hour as  a decimal  number using  a 12-hour  clock
          (range 01 to 12).

     %j   The day of  the year as a decimal number  (range 001 to
          366).

     %k   The hour (24-hour  clock) as a decimal  number (range 0
          to 23);  single digits are  preceded by a  blank.  (See
          also %H.)  (TZ)

     %l   The hour (12-hour  clock) as a decimal  number (range 1
          to 12);  single digits are  preceded by a  blank.  (See
          also %I.)  (TZ)

     %m   The month as a decimal number (range 01 to 12).

     %M   The minute as a decimal number (range 00 to 59).

     %n   A newline character. (SU)

     %O   Modifier: use alternative format, see below. (SU)

     %p   Either "AM" or "PM" according  to the given time value,
          or the  corresponding strings  for the  current locale.
          Noon is treated as "PM" and midnight as "AM".

     %P   Like  %p   but  in  lowercase:   "am"  or  "pm"   or  a
          corresponding string for the current locale. (GNU)

     %r   The time in a.m. or p.m. notation.  In the POSIX locale
          this is equivalent to %I:%M:%S %p.  (SU)

     %R   The  time  in  24-hour  notation (%H:%M).  (SU)  For  a
          version including the seconds, see %T below.

     %s   The  number  of  seconds since  the  Epoch,  1970-01-01
          00:00:00 +0000 (UTC). (TZ)

     %S   The second as a decimal  number (range 00 to 60).  (The
          range  is  up  to  60  to  allow  for  occasional  leap
          seconds.)

     %t   A tab character. (SU)

     %T   The time in 24-hour notation (%H:%M:%S). (SU)

     %u   The day of the week as  a decimal, range 1 to 7, Monday
          being 1.  See also %w.  (SU)

     %U   The  week  number of  the  current  year as  a  decimal
          number, range 00 to 53,  starting with the first Sunday
          as the first day of week 01.  See also %V and %W.

     %V   The  ISO 8601 week  number (see  NOTES) of  the current
          year as a decimal number, range  01 to 53, where week 1
          is the first  week that has at least 4  days in the new
          year.  See also %U and %W.  (SU)

     %w   The day of the week as  a decimal, range 0 to 6, Sunday
          being 0.  See also %u.

     %W   The  week  number of  the  current  year as  a  decimal
          number, range 00 to 53,  starting with the first Monday
          as the first day of week 01.

     %x   The  preferred  date  representation  for  the  current
          locale without the time.

     %X   The  preferred  time  representation  for  the  current
          locale without the date.

     %y   The year as  a decimal number without  a century (range
          00 to 99).

     %Y   The year as a decimal number including the century.

     %z   The +hhmm or -hhmm numeric  timezone (that is, the hour
          and minute offset from UTC). (SU)

     %Z   The timezone or name or abbreviation.

     %+   The  date  and  time   in  date(1)  format.  (TZ)  (Not
          supported in glibc2.)

     %%   A literal '%' character.

* Mon 02 Dec 2013 09:48:25 PM JST

class MyGmail(object):
    r"""
    """

    def __init__(self, from_=None, to=None, passwd=None):
        r"""

        @Arguments:
        - `passwd`:
        """
        self.FROM = from_
        self.TO = to
        self._passwd = passwd
        self._server = smtplib.SMTP('smtp.gmail.com', 587)
        self._server.ehlo()
        self._server.starttls()

    def login(self, user, passwd=None, delpass=True):
        r"""SUMMARY

        login(passwd=None)

        @Arguments:
        - `passwd`:

        @Return:
        """
        if passwd:
            self._passwd = passwd
        if not self._passwd:
            self._passwd = getpass('Input password: ')
        self._server.login(user, self._passwd)
        if delpass:
            self.delpassword()

    def delpassword(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        delpassword()

        @Return:
        """
        self._passwd = None

    def setfrom(self, from_):
        r"""SUMMARY

        setfrom(from_)

        @Arguments:
        - `from_`:

        @Return:
        """
        self.FROM = from_

    def setto(self, to):
        r"""SUMMARY

        setto(to)

        @Arguments:
        - `to`:

        @Return:
        """
        self.TO = to

    def send(self, msg, from_=None, to=None):
        r"""SUMMARY

        send()

        @Return:
        """
        if from_:
            self.setfrom(from_)
        if to:
            self.setto(to)
        self._server.sendmail(self.FROM, self.TO, msg)

(defun my-auto-insert-python ()
  (message "Select template: %s"
           (mapconcat
            (lambda (x)
              (cond
               ((not (string-match "\\S-" (nth 1 x)))
                (format "[%c]" (car x)))
               ((equal (downcase (car x))
                       (downcase (aref (nth 1 x) 0)))
                (format "[%c]%s" (car x)
                          (substring (nth 1 x) 1)))
               (t (format "[%c]%s" (car x) (nth 1 x)))))
              auto-insert-choose " "))
  (view-mode -1)
  (insert (car (cddr (assoc (read-char-exclusive) auto-insert-choose))))

* Tue 03 Dec 2013 12:14:58 PM JST
* syntax
    replacement_field ::=  "{" [field_name] ["!" conversion] [":" format_spec] "}"
    field_name        ::=  arg_name ("." attribute_name | "[" element_index "]")*
    arg_name          ::=  [identifier | integer]
    attribute_name    ::=  identifier
    element_index     ::=  integer | index_string
    index_string      ::=  <any source character except "]"> +
    conversion        ::=  "r" | "s" | "a"
    format_spec       ::=  <described in the next section>

* normal use
>>> a, b, d = 'google', 'yahoo', 'bing'
>>> "hello {0}, {1}, and {c}".format(a, b, c=d)
'hello google, yahoo, and bing'

>>> '{2}, {1}, {0}'.format('a', 'b', 'c')
'c, b, a'

>>> '{name} {age}'.format(age=18, name='hello')
'hello 18'

>>> '{name[1]}'.format(name=['hello', 'joe'])
'joe'

* Escape
>>> '{0} {{escaped}}'.format('joe')
'joe {escaped}'

* Adjust
>>> 'hello {0:8}'.format('joe')
'hello joe     '

>>> 'hello {0:{1}}'.format('yahoo', 8)
'hello yahoo   '

* Format specifier
# [[fill]align][sign][#][0][minimumwidth][.precision][type]
>>> 'google {0:<10}'.format('yahoo')
'google yahoo     '

>>> 'google {0:>10}'.format('yahoo')
'google      yahoo'

>>> 'google {0:^10}'.format('yahoo')
'google   yahoo   '

>>> 'google {0:*<10}'.format('yahoo')
'google yahoo*****'

>>> 'google {0:=>10}'.format('yahoo')
'google =====yahoo'

>>> 'google {0:?^10}'.format('yahoo')
'google ??yahoo???'

>>> 'hello {0:{1}{2}}'.format('yahoo', '>', 8)
'hello    yahoo'

>>> 'hello {0:=}'.format(8)
'hello 8'

>>> 'hello {0:=10}'.format(0.8)
'hello        0.8'

>>> 'hello {0:0=+10}'.format(0.8)
'hello +0000000.8'

>>> 'hello {0:0=-10}'.format(8)
'hello 0000000008'

>>> 'hello {0:>10s}'.format('8')
'hello          8'

>>> '{:,}'.format(1000000)
'1,000,000'


* '[]' (index)
>>> index = ['hello', 'world', 'hoge', 'foo', 'bar', 'yahoo', 'google', 'bing']
>>> '{[1]}'.format(index)
'world'

>>> '{0[1]}'.format(index)
'world'

* '.' (getattr) 
>>> '{.platform}'.format(sys)
'linux2'

>>> '{0.platform} {0.maxint}'.format(sys)
'linux2 2147483647'

>>> '{0.title} {1.title}'.format(w, ww)
'emacs@qu Inbox - takahiroatsumi0517@gmail.com - Icedove Mail/News'

* '[]' (getitem)
>>> '{0[name]} world'.format(dict(name='yahoo'))
'yahoo world'

>>> '{0[name]} world {0[age]}'.format(dict(name='yahoo', age=17))
'yahoo world 17'

* Explicit Conversion Flag !r, !s, !a
# !r - repr().
# !s - str().
# !a - ascii().
>>> '{0!r:20}'.format('hello\nworld')
"'hello\\nworld'      "

* ref
PEP3101 http://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-3101/
doc     http://docs.python.org/library/stdtypes.html#string-formatting-operations
http://docs.python.org/dev/library/string.html#formatstrings

#!/usr/bin/env python
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

# $Id$
# $Revision$
# $Date$
# $Author$
# $LastChangedBy$
# $LastChangedDate$

r"""Name: __init__.py


"""
import os
import sys
import xmlrpclib
import subprocess as _sbp
from multiprocessing import Pool

try:
	import pip
except ImportError, err:
	print(err)


__revision__ = "$Revision$"
__version__ = "0.1.0"

__all__ = [ '' ]

# for thread
OUTOFDATES = []


class OutofDate(object):
    r"""
    """

    def __init__(self, name, current, latest):
        r"""

        @Arguments:
        - `name`:
        - `latest`:
        - `current`:

        """
        self.name = name
        self.current = current
        self.latest = latest


def upgrade(name):
    r"""SUMMARY

    upgrade(name)

    @Arguments:
    - `name`:

    @Return:
    """
    try:
        _sbp.check_call(['pip', 'install', '--upgrade', name])
        return True
    except _sbp.CalledProcessError, err:
        return False
    # pip.main(['install', '--upgrade', name])

def get_outofdates():
    r"""SUMMARY

    get_outofdates()

    @Return:
    """
    global OUTOFDATES
    OUTOFDATES = []
    pool = Pool()
    poolmap = pool.map_async(comfirm_version, pip.get_installed_distributions())
    try:
        poolmap.get(0xFFFF)
        sys.stdout.flush()
        print '\n'
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        sys.stdout.flush()
        print '\n'
        print('Aborted')

    # pypi = xmlrpclib.ServerProxy("http://pypi.python.org/pypi")
    # outofdates = []
    # append = outofdates.append
    # for pkg in pip.get_installed_distributions():
    #     current = pkg.version
    #     latest = pypi.package_releases(pkg.project_name)
    #     if latest and not current == latest[0]:
    #         print('calc')
    #         append(OutofDate(pkg.project_name, current, latest[0]))

def comfirm_version(pkg):
    r"""SUMMARY

    comfirm_version(current, latest)

    @Arguments:
    - `current`:
    - `latest`:

    @Return:
    """
    global OUTOFDATES # for thread
    project_name = pkg.project_name
    os.write(1, '\rChecking {0:40}'.format(project_name))
    current = pkg.version
    pypi = xmlrpclib.ServerProxy("http://pypi.python.org/pypi")
    latest = pypi.package_releases(project_name)
    if latest and not current == latest[0]:
        OUTOFDATES.append(OutofDate(project_name, current, latest[0]))


def cli():
    r"""SUMMARY

    cli()

    @Return:
    """
    global OUTOFDATES
    get_outofdates()
    print(OUTOFDATES)
    try:
        numfmt = '{0:>{1}}) '
        leftfmt = '{0:<{1}}'
        centerfmt = '{0:<{1}}'
        while 1:
            listlen = len(OUTOFDATES)
            leftmax = max([len(x.name) for x in OUTOFDATES])
            centermax = max([len(x.current) for x in OUTOFDATES])
            numwide = len(str(listlen)) + 2 # digit len
            for i, pkg in enumerate(OUTOFDATES, start=1):
                stream = (numfmt.format(i, numwide) +
                          leftfmt.format(pkg.name, leftmax) +
                          centerfmt.format(pkg.current, centermax) +
                          '{0:^4}'.format('=>') +
                          pkg.latest)
                print(stream)
            print('\n' + numfmt.format(0, numwide) + ' exit\n')
            print(numfmt.format(00, numwide) + ' reflesh\n')
            menu_num = raw_input('input number >')
            if menu_num in ('0', 'exit'):
                sys.exit(os.EX_OK)
            if menu_num == '00':
                get_outofdates()
            if not menu_num:
                continue
            if listlen < int(menu_num):
                print('\nout of range {}\n'.format(menu_num))
                continue
            try:
                target = OUTOFDATES.pop(int(menu_num) - 1)
                print('upgrading {}'.format(target.name))
                upgrade(target.name)
            except KeyboardInterrupt:
                pass
            except:
                print('Fatal error')

    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        sys.exit(os.EX_OK)




# For Emacs
# Local Variables:
# coding: utf-8
# End:
# __init__.py ends here

* Tue 03 Dec 2013 02:33:49 PM JST
def _predef_options():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="""""")
    parser.add_argument('--version',
                        dest='version',
                        action='version',
                        version=__version__,
                        help='Version Strings.')
    # (yas/expand-link "argparse_add_argument" t)
    return parser

def _main():
    r"""Main function."""
    parser = _predef_options()
    opts = parser.parse_args()
    # parser.print_usage()
    cli()
    return os.EX_OK

if __name__ == '__main__':
    sys.exit(_main())

    def set_cc(self, cc_list):
        r"""SUMMARY

        set_cc(cc_list)

        @Arguments:
        - `cc_list`:

        @Return:
        """
        if predicate.isstring(cc_list):
            cc_list = [cc_list]
        if not type(cc_list) in (predicate.ListType, predicate.TupleType):
            raise ValueError('cc_list must be List or String type.')
        if self.cc:
            self.cc += cc_list
        else:
            self.cc = cc_list

(defvar flycheck-eval-after-load-hook nil
  "Hook for flycheck `eval-after-load'.")
(add-hook 'flycheck-eval-after-load-hook 'flycheck-mode-custom-predefine)
(add-hook 'flycheck-eval-after-load-hook 'flycheck-mode-predefine 'append)
(add-hook 'flycheck-eval-after-load-hook 'flycheck-mode-map-predefine 'append)
(add-hook 'flycheck-eval-after-load-hook 'flycheck-mode-face-predefine 'append)
(run-hooks-after-load "flycheck" 'flycheck-eval-after-load-hook)

;;;; flycheck
;;
;;;###autoload
(defun flycheck-mode-custom-predefine ()
  "For `eval-after-load' flycheck customize."
  (message "eval-after-load: \"flycheck\" customizing..")
  (custom-set-variables
   '(flycheck-highlighting-mode 'lines)
   '(flycheck-display-errors-delay 1.5)
   '(flycheck-idle-change-delay 1.0)
   '(flycheck-clang-language-standard "c++11"))
  )

;;;###autoload
(defun flycheck-mode-predefine ()
  "For `eval-after-load' flycheck function."
  (message "eval-after-load: \"flycheck\" setting..")
  (defun flycheck-may-check-buffer ()
    "Determine whether the buffer may be checked.
A buffer may not be checked under the following conditions:
- The buffer is read only (see `buffer-read-only').
Return t if the buffer may be checked and nil otherwise."
    (if (and buffer-file-name
             (not (re-in-string "\\.junk\\." buffer-file-name)))
        t
      nil))
  )

;;;###autoload
(defun flycheck-mode-map-predefine ()
  "For flycheck key bindings."
  (interactive)
  (unless (called-interactively-p 'interactive)
    (message "eval-after-load: \"flycheck\" keymaping.."))
  )

;;;###autoload
(defun flycheck-mode-face-predefine ()
  "For flycheck face."
  (message "eval-after-load: \"flycheck\" Setting faces..")
  ;; (face-spec-set 'flycheck-error-face   '((t :inherit flymake-errline)))
  ;; (face-spec-set 'flycheck-warning-face '((t :inherit flymake-warnline)))
  (face-spec-set 'flycheck-error
                 '((((class color) (background dark))
                    (:background "Firebrick4" :underline nil))
                   (((class color) (background light))
                    (:background "LightPink" :underline nil))
                   (t (:bold t))))

  (face-spec-set 'flycheck-warning
                 '((((class color) (background dark))
                    (:background "DarkBlue" :underline nil))
                   (((class color) (background light))
                    (:background "LightBlue2" :underline nil))
                   (t (:bold t :underline nil)))))

XKeyEvent createKeyEvent(Display *display, Window &win,
                           Window &winRoot, bool press,
                           int keycode, int modifiers)
{
   XKeyEvent event;

   event.display     = display;
   event.window      = win;
   event.root        = winRoot;
   event.subwindow   = None;
   event.time        = CurrentTime;
   event.x           = 1;
   event.y           = 1;
   event.x_root      = 1;
   event.y_root      = 1;
   event.same_screen = True;
   event.keycode     = XKeysymToKeycode(display, keycode);
   event.state       = modifiers;

   if(press)
      event.type = KeyPress;
   else
      event.type = KeyRelease;

   return event;
}

* Mon 16 Dec 2013 11:08:44 PM JST
#include <X11/Xlib.h>
#include <X11/keysym.h>

// The key code to be sent.
// A full list of available codes can be found in /usr/include/X11/keysymdef.h
#define KEYCODE XK_Down

// Function to create a keyboard event
XKeyEvent createKeyEvent(Display *display, Window &win,
                           Window &winRoot, bool press,
                           int keycode, int modifiers)
{
   XKeyEvent event;

   event.display     = display;
   event.window      = win;
   event.root        = winRoot;
   event.subwindow   = None;
   event.time        = CurrentTime;
   event.x           = 1;
   event.y           = 1;
   event.x_root      = 1;
   event.y_root      = 1;
   event.same_screen = True;
   event.keycode     = XKeysymToKeycode(display, keycode);
   event.state       = modifiers;

   if(press)
      event.type = KeyPress;
   else
      event.type = KeyRelease;

   return event;
}

main()
{
// Obtain the X11 display.
   Display *display = XOpenDisplay(0);
   if(display == NULL)
      return -1;

// Get the root window for the current display.
   Window winRoot = XDefaultRootWindow(display);

// Find the window which has the current keyboard focus.
   Window winFocus;
   int    revert;
   XGetInputFocus(display, &winFocus, &revert);

// Send a fake key press event to the window.
   XKeyEvent event = createKeyEvent(display, winFocus, winRoot, true, KEYCODE, 0);
   XSendEvent(event.display, event.window, True, KeyPressMask, (XEvent *)&event);

// Send a fake key release event to the window.
   event = createKeyEvent(display, winFocus, winRoot, false, KEYCODE, 0);
   XSendEvent(event.display, event.window, True, KeyPressMask, (XEvent *)&event);

// Done.
   XCloseDisplay(display);
   return 0;
}

XKeyEvent createKeyEvent(Display *display, Window &window,
                         Window &winRoot, bool press,
                         int keycode, int modifiers)
{
  XKeyEvent event;

  event.display = display;
  event.window  = window;
  event.root = winRoot;
  event.subwindow = None;
  event.time = CurrentTime;
  event.x = 1;
  event.y = 1;
  event.x_root = 1;
  event.y_root = 1;
  event.same_screen = True;
  event.keycode = XKeysymToKeycode(display, keycode);
  event.state = modifiers;
  if (press) {
    event.type = KeyPress;
  } else {
    event.type = KeyRelease;
  }
  return event;
}

void SendKeyEvent::sendKeyPress()
{
  XSendEvent(display, window, True, KeyPressMask, (XEvent *)&event);
}

void SendKeyEvent::sendKeyRelease()
{
  XSendEvent(display, window, True, KeyPressMask, (XEvent *)&event);
}


void SendKeyEvent::sendKey()
{
  sendKeyPress();
  sendKeyRelease();
}

void KeyEventHolder::createKeyEvent(bool press, int keycode, int modifiers)
{
  event.display     = display;
  event.window      = window;
  event.root        = root;
  event.subwindow   = None;
  event.time        = CurrentTime;
  event.x           = 1;
  event.y           = 1;
  event.x_root      = 1;
  event.y_root      = 1;
  event.same_screen = True;
  event.keycode     = XKeysymToKeycode(display, keycode);
  event.state       = modifiers;
  if (press) {
    event.type = KeyPress;
  } else {
    event.type = KeyRelease;
  }
}

* Tue 17 Dec 2013 05:38:50 AM JST
void KeyEventHolder::setWindow(Window win)
{
  event.window = win;
}


* Tue 17 Dec 2013 05:39:03 AM JST
void KeyEventHolder::setType(bool press)
{
  if (press) {
    event.type = KeyPress;
  } else {
    event.type = KeyRelease;
  }
}

void SendKey(int code, bool ctrl=False, bool alt=False, bool shift=False,
             bool super=False)
{
  // press modifiers
  if (ctrl)
    XTestFakeKeyEvent(display, XKeysymToKeycode(display, XK_Control_L), true, 0);
  if (alt)
    XTestFakeKeyEvent(display, XKeysymToKeycode(display, XK_Alt_L), true, 0);
  if (shift)
    XTestFakeKeyEvent(display, XKeysymToKeycode(display, XK_Shift_L), true, 0);
  if (super)
    XTestFakeKeyEvent(display, XKeysymToKeycode(display, XK_Super_L), true, 0);
  
  // send key
  XTestFakeKeyEvent(display, XKeysymToKeycode(display, code), true, 0);
  XTestFakeKeyEvent(display, XKeysymToKeycode(display, code), false, 0);
  
  // release modifiers
  if (ctrl)
    XTestFakeKeyEvent(display, XKeysymToKeycode(display, XK_Control_L), false, 0);
  if (alt)
    XTestFakeKeyEvent(display, XKeysymToKeycode(display, XK_Alt_L), false, 0);
  if (shift)
    XTestFakeKeyEvent(display, XKeysymToKeycode(display, XK_Shift_L), false, 0);
  if (super)
    XTestFakeKeyEvent(display, XKeysymToKeycode(display, XK_Super_L), false, 0);
  
}

bool Main::handle() {
  // std::cout << "in handle" << std::endl;
  while (XPending(display)) {
      XEvent ev;
      XNextEvent(display, &ev);
      handle_event(ev);
  }
  return true;
}

std::string KeyMap::get(int key)
{
  auto value = keymap.find(key);
  return value != keymap.end() ? value->second : "";
}

#include <cairo.h>
#include <cairo-xlib.h>
#include <X11/Xlib.h>

int main(int argc, char** argv) {
    Display *disp;
    Window root;
    cairo_surface_t *surface;
    int scr;

    disp = XOpenDisplay(NULL);
    scr = DefaultScreen(disp);
    root = DefaultRootWindow(disp);

    surface = cairo_xlib_surface_create(disp, root, DefaultVisual(disp, scr),
            DisplayWidth(disp, scr), DisplayHeight(disp, scr));
    cairo_surface_write_to_png(
            surface,
            "test.png");
    cairo_surface_destroy(surface);

    return 0;
}

#!/usr/bin/env python
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""JUNK"""
import os
import sys
import re

from evdev import InputDevice, ecodes, categorize
from select import select


class KeyMap(dict):
    r"""
    """

    def __init__(self, ):
        r"""
        """
        dumpkeys = os.popen('dumpkeys').readlines()
        keyre = re.compile('keycode[\s]*([0-9]*) = ([\S]*)')
        for line in dumpkeys:
            result = keyre.search(line)
            if result:
                keycode, char = result.groups()
                self.update({keycode:char})

import os
import sys
import re

from evdev import InputDevice, ecodes, categorize
from select import select


class KeyMap(dict):
    r"""
    """

    def __init__(self, ):
        r"""
        """
        dumpkeys = os.popen('dumpkeys').readlines()
        keyre = re.compile('keycode[\s]*([0-9]*) = ([\S]*)')
        for line in dumpkeys:
            result = keyre.search(line)
            if result:
                keycode, char = result.groups()
                self.update({keycode:char})

        r"""

* Sat 21 Dec 2013 06:36:18 PM JST
def auto_get_event_devices():
    r"""SUMMARY

    auto_get_event_device()

    @Return:
    """
    standard_path = '/dev/input'
    events = []
    append = events.append
    for ntuple in ParseDevices():
        if ntuple.EV == KEYBOARD:
            match = re.search('event[0-9]+', ntuple.Handlers)
            if match:
                append(os.path.join(standard_path, match.group()))
    return events

class KeyMap(dict):
    r"""
    """
    _rename_map = {'one':  '1',
                   'two':  '2',
                   'three': '3',
                   'four': '4',
                   'five': '5',
                   'fix': '6',
                   'seven': '7',
                   'eight':  '8',
                   'nine':  '9',
                   'zero':  '0',
                   'ntilde':  'ñ',
                   'comma':  ',',
                   'minus':  '-',
                   'space':  ' ',
                   'period':  '.',
                   'colon': ':',
                   'semicolon': ';',
                   }
    _special_fmt = '<{}>'

    def __init__(self, ):
        r"""
        """
        dumpkeys = os.popen('dumpkeys --keys-only --separate-lines').readlines()
        for line in dumpkeys:
            if not line.startswith(('plain')):
                continue
            # 'plain\tkeycode 255 = VoidSymbol '
            # => ['plain\tkeycode', '255', '=', 'VoidSymbol']
            _, keycode, _, char, _ = [x for x in line.split(' ') if not x == '']
            if char.startswith(('+')):
                char = char[1:]
            elif char in self._rename_map:
                char = self._rename_map[char]
            elif char == 'VoidSymbol':
                char = ''
            else:
                char = self._special_fmt.format(char)
            self[int(keycode)] = char

class _YearMeta(type):
    r"""Singleton."""

    def __new__(cls, name, bases, dict):
        dict['_instances'] = {}
        return type.__new__(cls, name, bases, dict)

    def __call__(self, *args):
        if not args:
            args = (_date.today().year, )
        if not args in self._instances:
            self._instances[args] = type.__call__(self, args)
        return self._instances[args]

class UnpackError(Exception):
    r"""
    """

    def __init__(self, klass):
        r"""

        @Arguments:
        - `klass`:
        """
        self._klass = klass

    def __str__(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        __str__()

        @Return:
        """
        return self._klass.message

class DumpKeys(Singleton):
    r"""Buffering key by dumpkeys command.

    This class is Singleton.
    command line: 'dumpkeys --keys-only --separate-lines'
    and iterable like this.
    for line in DumpKeys():
        print(line)
    """
    _cmdline = 'dumpkeys --keys-only --separate-lines'

    def __init__(self, ):
        self.lines = os.popen(self._cmdline).readlines()

    def __iter__(self, ):
        for line in self.lines:
            yield line

class KeyMap(DictUtil):
    r"""Plain keymap dictionary <int, str>.

    @Arguments:
    - `voidsymbol`: replace 'VoidSymbol' string.
    """
    _rename_map = RENAME_MAP
    _special_fmt = SPECIAL_KEY_FMT
    _regexp = '^plain'

    def __init__(self, voidsymbol=''):
        self.voidsymbol = voidsymbol
        self._parse_dumpkeys()

    def reload(self, ):
        r"""Reload keymap.

        reload()
        """
        self.delete_all()
        self._parse_dumpkeys()

    def _parse_dumpkeys(self, ):
        r"""Parse and set dictionary keycode, char from dumpkeys.

        _parse_dumpkeys()
        """
        for line in self._iter_lines():
            keycode, char = self._parse_line(line)
            char = self._filter_char(char)
            self.setmap(keycode, char)

    def _iter_lines(self, ):
        r"""Generator each matched line from dumpkeys command.

        _iter_lines()

        @Return:
        yield line.
        """
        for line in DumpKeys():
            if self._ismatch_line(line):
                yield line

    def _ismatch_line(self, line):
        r"""Check matched line.

        _ismatch_line(line)

        @Arguments:
        - `line`: target statements

        @Return:
        None, if not matched.
        match object, if matched.
        """
        return re.search(self._regexp, line)

    def _parse_line(self, line):
        r"""Parse keycode and char from line.

        _parse_line(line)

        @Arguments:
        - `line`: (str)

        @Return:
        int, str

        Split statements to list by space.
        'plain\tkeycode 255 = VoidSymbol\n'
        => ['plain\tkeycode', '255', '=', 'VoidSymbol', '\n']
        """
        try:
            _, keycode, _, char, _ = [x for x in line.split(' ') if not x == '']
        except ValueError, err:
            raise UnpackError(err)
        return keycode, char

    def _filter_char(self, char):
        r"""Filtering char.

        _filter_char(char)

        @Arguments:
        - `char`: (str)

        @Return:
        str
        """
        if char.startswith(('+')):
            char = char[1:]
        elif char in self._rename_map:
            char = self._rename_map[char]
        elif char == 'VoidSymbol':
            char = self.voidsymbol
        else:
            char = self._special_fmt.format(char)
        return char

    def setmap(self, keycode, char):
        r"""Alternative set dictionary for this.

        setmap(keycode, char)

        @Arguments:
        - `keycode`: int
        - `char`: str
        """
        self[int(keycode)] = char


class KeyUpMap(KeyMap):
    r"""For Key up dictionary."""
    _special_fmt = SPECIAL_UPKEY_FMT


class KeyShiftMap(KeyMap):
    r"""For Modifier key shift dictionary."""
    _special_fmt = SPECIAL_KEY_FMT
    _regexp = r'^[\t\s]+shift[\t\s]+keycode'

class UnpackError(Exception):
    r"""Unpack Exception."""

    def __init__(self, klass):
        super(UnpackError, self).__init__(klass)
        self._klass = klass

    def __str__(self, ):
        return self._klass.message

* Sun 22 Dec 2013 11:59:20 PM JST
    def run(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        run()

        @Return:
        """
        try:
            device = InputDevice(self._device)
            self.file = open(self._filename, 'a')
            while 1:
                _, _, _ = select([device], [], [])
                for event in device.read():
                    if event.type == ecodes.EV_KEY:
                        # key up
                        if event.value == KeyLogger._key_up:
                            action = self.handle_up(event)
                        # shift key
                        elif self._shift:
                            action = self.handle_shift(event)
                        # key hold
                        elif event.value == KeyLogger._key_hold:
                            action = self.handle_hold(event)
                        # down
                        elif event.value == KeyLogger._key_down:
                            action = self.handle_down(event)
                        # do action
                        if action == self._continue:
                            continue
                        elif action == self._break:
                            break
                        # write out
                        self.write()
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            print('\n\nKeylogger Keyboard interrupted.')
        finally:
            self.file.close()
            device.close()

    def list_kbd_evdev(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        list_kbd_evdev()

        @Return:
        """
        edevs = []
        append = edevs.append
        for ntuple in self.ntuples:
            if ntuple.EV == KEYBOARD:
                match = re.search(self._regexp, ntuple.Handlers)
                if match:
                    append(os.path.join(self._stdpath, match.group(),))
        return edevs

    def get_kbd_evdev(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        get_kbd_evdev()

        @Return:
        """
        edevs = self.list_kbd_evdev()
        if edevs:
            return edevs[0]
        return None

    def handle_up(self, event):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_up()

        @Return:
        """
        self.str = self._upkeymap[event.code]
        if self.str == r'<\Shift>':
            self._shift = False
            self.str = ''
        if not self.str in (r'<\Alt>', r'<\Control>'):
            self.str = ''

    def syn_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_SYN.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        syn_event(event)

        Used as markers to separate events. Events may be separated in time or
        in space, such as with the multitouch protocol.
        """
        pass

    def key_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_KEY.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        ev_key(event)

        Used to describe state changes of keyboards, buttons, or other key-like
        devices.
        """
        pass

    def rel_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_REL.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        rel_event(event)

        Used to describe relative axis value changes,
        e.g. moving the mouse 5 units to the left.
        """
        pass

    def abs_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_ABS.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        abs_event(event)

        Used to describe absolute axis value changes, e.g. describing the
        coordinates of a touch on a touchscreen.
        """
        pass

    def msc_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle MSC_EV.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        msc_event(event)

        Used to describe miscellaneous input data that
        do not fit into other types.
        """
        pass

    def sw_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_SE.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        sw_event(event)

        Used to describe binary state input switches.
        """
        pass

    def led_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_LED.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        led_event(event)

        Used to turn LEDs on devices on and off.
        """
        pass

    def snd_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_SND.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        snd_event(event)

        Used to output sound to devices.
        """
        pass

    def rep_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_REP.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        rep_event(event)

        Used for autorepeating devices.
        """
        pass

    def ff_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_FF.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        ff_event(event)

        Used to send force feedback commands to an input device.
        """
        pass

    def pwr_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_PWR.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        pwr_event(event)

        A special type for power button and switch input.
        """
        pass

    def ff_status_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_FF_STATUS.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        ff_status_event(event)

        Used to receive force feedback device status.
        """
        pass

* Mon 23 Dec 2013 07:40:30 AM JST
    def handle_branch(self, event):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_branch(event)

        @Arguments:
        - `event`:

        @Return:
        """
        if event.type == ecodes.EV_SYN:
            self.syn_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_KEY:
            self.key_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_REL:
            self.rel_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_ABS:
            self.abs_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_MSC:
            self.msc_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_SW:
            self.sw_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_LED:
            self.led_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_SND:
            self.snd_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_REP:
            self.rep_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_FF:
            self.ff_event(event)
        elif event.type_ == ecodes.EV_PWR:
            self.pwr_event(event)
        elif event.type_ == ecodes.EV_FF_STATUS:
            self.ff_status_event(event)

* Mon 23 Dec 2013 07:44:54 AM JST
    def handle(self, ):
        r"""Handle event from input devices.

        @Return:
        None

        handle()

        Infinity loop read event from input devices.
        And execute each event handler.
        """
        while 1:
            rlist, _, _ = select(self.readdevs, [], [])
            for inputdev in rlist:
                for event in inputdev.read():
                    self.handle_branch(event)

    def wait_io(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        wait_io()

        @Return:
        """
        rlist, _, _ = select(self.readdevs, [], [])
        return rlist

class Select(object):
    r"""
    """
    __metaclass__ = ABCMeta

    def __init__(self, rlist, wlist, xlist, timeout=0):
        r"""

        @Arguments:
        - `rlist`:
        - `wlist`:
        - `xlist`:
        - `timeout`:
        """
        self.rlist = rlist
        self.wlist = wlist
        self.xlist = xlist
        self.timeout = timeout

    def wait_io(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        wait_io()

        @Return:
        """
        return select.select(self.rlist, self.wlist, self.xlist, self.timeout)

    def handle_io(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_io()

        @Return:
        """
        while 1:
            try:
                rlist, wlist, xlist = self.wait_io()
            except select.error, err:
                print(err)
                break
            except IOError, err:
                print(err)
                break
            # rlist
            for obj in rlist:
                self.handle_read(obj)
                # for event in io_obj.read():
                    # self.event_branch(event)
            # wlist
            for obj in wlist:
                self.handle_write(obj)
                # for event in io_obj.read():
                    # self.event_branch(event)
            # xlist
            for obj in xlist:
                self.handle_except(obj)
                # for event in io_obj.read():
                    # self.event_branch(event)

    @abstractmethod
    def handle_read(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_read(io_obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `io_obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        raise NotImplementedError

    @abstractmethod
    def handle_write(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_write(io_obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `io_obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        raise NotImplementedError

    @abstractmethod
    def handle_except(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_except(io_obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `io_obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        raise NotImplementedError

    def handle_event(self, ):
        """Handle infinitey.

        OVERRIDE: like this.
        def handle(self, ):
            while 1:
                rlist, _, _ = select(self.fileobjs, [], [])
                for inputdev in rlist:
                    for event in inputdev.read():
                        self.event_branch(event)
        """
        self.handle_io()

    def event_branch(self, event):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_branch(event)

        @Arguments:
        - `event`:

        @Return:
        """
        if event.type == ecodes.EV_SYN:
            self.syn_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_KEY:
            self.key_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_REL:
            self.rel_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_ABS:
            self.abs_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_MSC:
            self.msc_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_SW:
            self.sw_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_LED:
            self.led_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_SND:
            self.snd_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_REP:
            self.rep_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_FF:
            self.ff_event(event)
        elif event.type_ == ecodes.EV_PWR:
            self.pwr_event(event)
        elif event.type_ == ecodes.EV_FF_STATUS:
            self.ff_status_event(event)

class SelectABC(object):
    r"""
    """
    __metaclass__ = ABCMeta

    def __init__(self, rlist, wlist, xlist, timeout=0):
        r"""

        @Arguments:
        - `rlist`:
        - `wlist`:
        - `xlist`:
        - `timeout`:
        """
        self.rlist = rlist
        self.wlist = wlist
        self.xlist = xlist
        self.timeout = timeout

    def wait_io(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        wait_io()

        @Return:
        """
        return select.select(self.rlist, self.wlist, self.xlist, self.timeout)

    def handle_io(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_io()

        @Return:
        """
        while 1:
            try:
                rlist, wlist, xlist = self.wait_io()
            except select.error, err:
                print(err)
                break
            except IOError, err:
                print(err)
                break
            # rlist
            if rlist: # for fast
                for obj in rlist:
                    self.handle_read(obj)
            # wlist
            if wlist: # for fast
                for obj in wlist:
                    self.handle_write(obj)
            # xlist
            if xlist: # for fast
                for obj in xlist:
                    self.handle_except(obj)

    @abstractmethod
    def handle_read(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_read(io_obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `io_obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        raise NotImplementedError

    @abstractmethod
    def handle_write(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_write(io_obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `io_obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        raise NotImplementedError

    @abstractmethod
    def handle_except(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_except(io_obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `io_obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        raise NotImplementedError

* Mon 23 Dec 2013 12:21:30 PM JST
    def __init__(self, rlist, wlist, xlist, timeout=0):
        r"""SUMMARY

        __init__(rlist, wlist, xlist, timeout=0)

        @Arguments:
        - `rlist`:
        - `wlist`:
        - `xlist`:
        - `timeout`:

        @Return:
        """
        super(EventHandlerABC, self).__init__(rlist, wlist, xlist,
                                              timeout=timeout)

    def handle_event(self, ):
        """Handle infinitey.
        """
        self.handle_io()

    def hendle_read(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        hendle_read(obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        for event in obj.read():
            self.event_branch(event)

    def handle_write(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_write(obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        for event in obj.read():
            self.event_branch(event)

    def handle_except(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_except(obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        for event in obj.read():
            self.event_branch(event)

#!/usr/bin/env python
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""JUNK"""
import os
import sys
import re

import evdev

KEY_DOWN = 1
KEY_UP = 0
KEY_HOLD = 2


def sendkey(ui, key, ctrl=False, alt=False, shift=False):
    r"""SUMMARY

    sendkey()

    @Return:
    """
    if ctrl:
        ui.write(evdev.ecodes.EV_KEY, evdev.ecodes.KEY_LEFTCTRL, KEY_DOWN)
    if alt:
        ui.write(evdev.ecodes.EV_KEY, evdev.ecodes.KEY_LEFTALT, KEY_DOWN)
    if shift:
        ui.write(evdev.ecodes.EV_KEY, evdev.ecodes.KEY_LEFTSHIFT, KEY_DOWN)

    ui.write(evdev.ecodes.EV_KEY, key, KEY_DOWN)
    ui.write(evdev.ecodes.EV_KEY, key, KEY_UP)

    if ctrl:
        ui.write(evdev.ecodes.EV_KEY, evdev.ecodes.KEY_LEFTCTRL, KEY_UP)
    if alt:
        ui.write(evdev.ecodes.EV_KEY, evdev.ecodes.KEY_LEFTALT, KEY_UP)
    if shift:
        ui.write(evdev.ecodes.EV_KEY, evdev.ecodes.KEY_LEFTSHIFT, KEY_UP)

class KeyMaps(object):
    r"""Key Maps."""

    def __init__(self, ):
        self._keymap = KeyMap()
        self._shiftmap = KeyShiftMap()
        self._keyupmap = KeyUpMap()

    def getkey(self, keycode):
        r"""SUMMARY

        getkey(keycode)

        @Arguments:
        - `keycode`:

        @Return:
        """
        return self._keymap.get(keycode, '')

    def getshiftkey(self, keycode):
        r"""SUMMARY

        getshiftkey(keycode)

        @Arguments:
        - `keycode`:

        @Return:
        """
        return self._shiftmap.get(keycode, '')

    def getupkey(self, keycode):
        r"""SUMMARY

        getupkey(keycode)

        @Arguments:
        - `keycode`:

        @Return:
        """
        return self._keyupmap.get(keycode, '')

class EventDevice(object):
    r"""Event Device."""
    _stdpath = '/dev/input'
    _regexp = 'event[0-9]+'

    def __init__(self, stdpath=None, regexp=None):
        r"""
        """
        self._stdpath = stdpath or self._stdpath
        self._regexp = regexp or self._regexp
        self.ntuples = get_devices_info()


class EventKBDDevice(EventDevice):
    r"""Event KeyBoard Device."""

    def __init__(self, device=None, stdpath=None, regexp=None):
        if device:
            self._device = device
        else: # auto dev
            super(EventKBDDevice, self).__init__(stdpath=stdpath, regexp=regexp)
            self._device = self.get_kbd_evdev()
        if not self._device:
            raise NoEventDevice()

    def list_kbd_evdev(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        list_kbd_evdev()

        @Return:
        """
        edevs = []
        append = edevs.append
        for ntuple in self.ntuples:
            if ntuple.EV == KEYBOARD:
                match = re.search(self._regexp, ntuple.Handlers)
                if match:
                    append(os.path.join(self._stdpath, match.group(),))
        return edevs

    def get_kbd_evdev(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        get_kbd_evdev()

        @Return:
        """
        edevs = self.list_kbd_evdev()
        if edevs:
            return edevs[0]
        return None

class EventHandlerAbstract(object):
    r"""

    ref. 'https://www.kernel.org/doc/Documentation/input/event-codes.txt'
    """

    def event_branch(self, event):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_branch(event)

        @Arguments:
        - `event`:

        @Return:
        """
        if event.type == ecodes.EV_SYN:
            self.syn_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_KEY:
            self.key_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_REL:
            self.rel_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_ABS:
            self.abs_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_MSC:
            self.msc_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_SW:
            self.sw_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_LED:
            self.led_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_SND:
            self.snd_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_REP:
            self.rep_event(event)
        elif event.type == ecodes.EV_FF:
            self.ff_event(event)
        elif event.type_ == ecodes.EV_PWR:
            self.pwr_event(event)
        elif event.type_ == ecodes.EV_FF_STATUS:
            self.ff_status_event(event)

    def syn_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_SYN.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        syn_event(event)

        Used as markers to separate events. Events may be separated in time or
        in space, such as with the multitouch protocol.
        """
        pass

    def key_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_KEY.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        ev_key(event)

        Used to describe state changes of keyboards, buttons, or other key-like
        devices.
        """
        pass

    def rel_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_REL.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        rel_event(event)

        Used to describe relative axis value changes,
        e.g. moving the mouse 5 units to the left.
        """
        pass

    def abs_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_ABS.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        abs_event(event)

        Used to describe absolute axis value changes, e.g. describing the
        coordinates of a touch on a touchscreen.
        """
        pass

    def msc_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle MSC_EV.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        msc_event(event)

        Used to describe miscellaneous input data that
        do not fit into other types.
        """
        pass

    def sw_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_SE.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        sw_event(event)

        Used to describe binary state input switches.
        """
        pass

    def led_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_LED.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        led_event(event)

        Used to turn LEDs on devices on and off.
        """
        pass

    def snd_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_SND.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        snd_event(event)

        Used to output sound to devices.
        """
        pass

    def rep_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_REP.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        rep_event(event)

        Used for autorepeating devices.
        """
        pass

    def ff_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_FF.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        ff_event(event)

        Used to send force feedback commands to an input device.
        """
        pass

    def pwr_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_PWR.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        pwr_event(event)

        A special type for power button and switch input.
        """
        pass

    def ff_status_event(self, event):
        r"""Handle EV_FF_STATUS.

        @Arguments:
        - `event`: event object

        @Return:
        None

        ff_status_event(event)

        Used to receive force feedback device status.
        """
        pass


class EventHandler(EventHandlerAbstract, SelectABC):
    r"""Event Handler."""

    def __init__(self, rlist, wlist, xlist, timeout=0):
        r"""SUMMARY

        __init__(rlist, wlist, xlist, timeout=0)

        @Arguments:
        - `rlist`:
        - `wlist`:
        - `xlist`:
        - `timeout`:

        @Return:
        """
        super(EventHandler, self).__init__(rlist, wlist, xlist, timeout=timeout)

    def handle_event(self, ):
        """Handle infinitey.
        """
        self.handle_io()

    def handle_read(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        hendle_read(obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        for event in obj.read():
            self.event_branch(event)

    def handle_write(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_write(obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        for event in obj.read():
            self.event_branch(event)

    def handle_except(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_except(obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        for event in obj.read():
            self.event_branch(event)


class EventKeyABC(object):
    r"""Event Key ABC.

    EV_KEY
    """
    __metaclass__ = ABCMeta

    _key_up = 0
    _key_down = 1
    _key_hold = 2

    def key_event(self, event):
        r"""SUMMARY

        key_event(event)

        @Arguments:
        - `event`:

        @Return:
        """
        # key up
        if self._key_up == event.value:
            self.keyup(event)
        # key hold
        elif self._key_hold == event.value:
            self.keyhold(event)
        # down
        elif self._key_down == event.value:
            self.keydown(event)

    @abstractmethod
    def keyup(self, event):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_up(event)

        @Arguments:
        - `event`:

        @Return:
        """
        raise NotImplementedError()

    @abstractmethod
    def keyhold(self, event):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_hold(event)

        @Arguments:
        - `event`:

        @Return:
        """
        raise NotImplementedError()

    @abstractmethod
    def keydown(self, event):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_down(event)

        @Arguments:
        - `event`:

        @Return:
        """
        raise NotImplementedError()

    def key_event(self, event):
        r"""SUMMARY

        key_event(event)

        @Arguments:
        - `event`:

        @Return:
        """
        # key up
        if event.value == KeyLogger._key_up:
            self.keyup(event)
        # shift key
        elif self._shift:
            self.keyshift(event)
        # key hold
        elif event.value == KeyLogger._key_hold:
            self.keyhold(event)
        # down
        elif event.value == KeyLogger._key_down:
            self.keydown(event)
        # write out
        if self.str:
            self.write()

    def key_event(self, event):
        r"""SUMMARY

        key_event(event)

        @Arguments:
        - `event`:

        @Return:
        """
        # key up
        if event.value == KeyLogger._key_up:
            self.keyup(event)
        # shift key

        # key hold

            self.keyhold(event)
        # down
        elif event.value == KeyLogger._key_down:
            self.keydown(event)
        # write out
        if self.str:
            self.write()

class DumpKeys(Singleton):
    r"""Buffering key by dumpkeys command.

    This class is Singleton.
    command line: 'dumpkeys --keys-only --separate-lines'
    and iterable like this.
    for line in DumpKeys():
        print(line)
    """
    _cmdline = 'dumpkeys --keys-only --separate-lines'

    def __init__(self, ):
        self.lines = _os.popen(self._cmdline).readlines()

    def __iter__(self, ):
        for line in self.lines:
            yield line

class KeyState(object):
    r"""
    """
    _keyup = 0
    _keydown = 1
    _keyhold = 2

    def __init__(self, value):
        r"""

        @Arguments:
        - `value`:
        """
        self._value = value

    def iskeyup(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        iskeyup()

        @Return:
        """
        return self._value == self._keyup

    def iskeydown(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        iskeydown()

        @Return:
        """
        return self._value == self._keydown

    def iskeyhold(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        iskeyhold()

        @Return:
        """
        return self._value == self._keyhold

class KeyCodeState(KeyState, KeyCode):
    r"""
    """

    def __init__(self, code, value):
        r"""

        @Arguments:
        - `code`:
        - `value`:
        """
        KeyState.__init__(code)
        KeyCode.__init__(value)

    @property
    def keystring(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        keystring()

        @Return:
        """
        # return map.get()

    def getmatchkeys(self, value):
        r"""SUMMARY

        getmatchkeys(vlaue)

        @Arguments:
        - `vlaue`:

        @Return:
        """
        results = []
        for key, val in self.iteritems():
            if value == val:
                results.append(key)
        return results

    def is_shift_hold(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY
        
        is_shift_hold()
        
        @Return:
        """
        for code in self.shiftkeys:
            if code in self.holdkeys:
                return True
        return False

class KeyHoldHandler(_KeyHoldHandlerABC):
    r"""
    """

    def handle(self, event):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle(event)

        @Arguments:
        - `event`:

        @Return:
        """
        event.hold()


* Sun 29 Dec 2013 01:21:33 AM JST
class KeyDownHandler(_KeyDownHandlerABC):
    r"""
    """

    def handle(self, event):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle(event)

        @Arguments:
        - `event`:

        @Return:
        """
        if event.scancode in event.modkeys:
            event.hold()
        if event.scancode in event.shiftkeys:
            return
        if event.is_shift_hold():
            print(KEYMAPS.getshiftkey(event.scancode))
        else:
            print(KEYMAPS.getkey(event.scancode))


* Sun 29 Dec 2013 01:21:47 AM JST

class KeyUpHandler(_KeyUpHandlerABC):
    r"""
    """

    def handle(self, event):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle(event)

        @Arguments:
        - `event`:

        @Return:
        """
        event.unhold()
        if event.scancode in event.shiftkeys:
            return
        if event.scancode in event.modkeys:
            print(KEYMAPS.getupkey(event.scancode))

        # if event.shiftkey in event.holdkeys:
        #     print('DEBUG-1-dispacher.py')
        #     print(KEYMAPS.getupkey(event.scancode))
        # print('key up!!')
        # print(event.keystring)
        # print(event.holdkeys)

class SelectInputDeviceABC(SelectABC):
    r"""
    """

    def __init__(self, device=None):
        r"""

        @Arguments:
        - `device`:
        """
        self._device = device
        self.readlist = self._setdevices()
        SelectABC.__init__(self, rlist=self.readlist, wlist=(), xlist=())

    def _setdevices(self, device=None):
        r"""SUMMARY

        _setdevices(device=None)

        @Arguments:
        - `device`:

        @Return:
        """
        readlist = []
        if predicate.isstring(device):
            readlist.append(AutoKBDInputDevice(device))
        elif device is None:
            for dev in evdev.list_devices():
                readlist.append(evdev.InputDevice(dev))
        else:
            for dev in device:
                readlist.append(evdev.InputDevice(dev))
        return readlist

class SetDevice(object):
    r"""
    """

    def __init__(self, device=None):
        r"""

        @Arguments:
        - `device`:
        """
        self._device = device
        readlist = []
        if predicate.isstring(device):
            readlist.append(AutoKBDInputDevice(device))
        elif device is None:
            for dev in evdev.list_devices():
                readlist.append(evdev.InputDevice(dev))
        else:
            for dev in device:
                readlist.append(evdev.InputDevice(dev))
        self.readlist = readlist

def xfce_launch():
    r"""SUMMARY

    xfce_launch()

    @Return:
    """
    if wm.exists(klass='Xfrun4'):
        win = wm.getwin(klass='Xfrun4')
        if win:
            win.close()
    else:
        active_win = wm.active.ActiveWindow()
        if not 'Emacs' in active_win.klass:
            _sbp.Popen(['xfrun4'])

    def _init_handler(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        _init_handler()

        @Return:
        """
        for klass in self._keyhandlers:
            inst = klass(self.fileobj)
            self._keyhandler_map.update({inst.KEYVALUE: inst.handle})
        eventkeyhandler = EventKeyHandler(dic=self._keyhandler_map)
        handler = EventHandler(dic={
            eventkeyhandler.keyword: eventkeyhandler.do})
        return handler

    def run(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        run()

        @Return:
        """
        try:
            self.handle_io()
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            print('\n\nKeylogger Keyboard interrupted.')

    def handle_read(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_read(obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        for event in obj.read():
            self.handler.do(key=event.type, event=event)

    def handle_write(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_write(obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        pass

    def handle_except(self, obj):
        r"""SUMMARY

        handle_except(obj)

        @Arguments:
        - `obj`:

        @Return:
        """
        pass

* Mon 30 Dec 2013 01:47:37 PM JST
    def download(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        download()

        @Return:
        """
        html = self._download_project()
        if html:
            self._download_signature()
        return html

    def _download_project(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        _download_project()

        @Return:
        """
        html = gethtml(self.simple_url)
        if not html:
            return None
        if not path.exists(self.simple_dir):
            os.mkdir(self.simple_dir)
        savefile(self.simple_index_path, html)
        return html

    def _download_signature(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        download_signature()

        @Return:
        """
        html = gethtml(self.signature_url)
        if not html:
            return None
        savefile(self.signature_path, html)

class Projects(object):
    r"""
    """
    _baseurl = SIMPLE_URL

    def __init__(self, project, basedir):
        r"""

        @Arguments:
        - `project`:
        - `basedir`:
        """
        self._project = project
        self._basedir = basedir

    @property
    def simple_url(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        simple_url()

        @Return:
        """
        url = urlparse.urljoin(self._baseurl, urllib2.quote(self._project))
        if not url.endswith(('/')):
            url += '/'
        return url

    @property
    def simple_url(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        simple_url()

        @Return:
        """
        url = urlparse.urljoin(self._baseurl, urllib2.quote(self._name))
        if not url.endswith(('/')):
            url += '/'
        return url

* Tue 31 Dec 2013 03:44:35 AM JST
            try:
                pkgobj = Package(pkg)
                pkgdir = path.join(self.archive_dir, pkgobj.name)
                osutil.safe_mkdir(pkgdir)
                url = pkgobj.get_latest_url()
                if not url:
                    continue
                print('Downloaded {}'.format(url))
                filename = url.split('/')[-1]
                dest = path.join(pkgdir, filename)
                download(url, dest)
                pip.util.unpack_file(dest, self.source_dir, '', '')
                print('Successed {}\n\n'.format(dest))
            except KeyboardInterrupt:
                sys.exit(os.EX_OK)
            except:
                print('!!! Failed {}\n\n'.format(pkg))

       def ascii_to_bin(char):                                                                                          
       ascii = ord(char)                                                                                                
       bin = []                                                                                                         
                                                                                                                        
       while (ascii > 0):                                                                                               
       if (ascii & 1) == 1:                                                                                             
       bin.append("1")                                                                                                  
       else:                                                                                                            
       bin.append("0")                                                                                                  
       ascii = ascii >> 1                                                                                               
                                                                                                                        
       bin.reverse()                                                                                                    
       binary = "".join(bin)                                                                                            
       zerofix = (8 - len(binary)) * '0'                                                                                
                                                                                                                        
       return zerofix + binary

def ascii_to_bin(char):
    ascii = ord(char)
    bin = []
    while (ascii > 0):
        if (ascii & 1) == 1:
            bin.append("1")
        else:
            bin.append("0")
        ascii = ascii >> 1

    bin.reverse()
    binary = "".join(bin)
    zerofix = (8 - len(binary)) * '0'
    return zerofix + binary

* Tue 31 Dec 2013 05:29:39 AM JST
def ascii_to_bin(char):
    ascii = ord(char)
    bin = []
    while (ascii > 0):
        if (ascii & 1) == 1:
            bin.append("1")
        else:
            bin.append("0")
        ascii = ascii >> 1

    bin.reverse()
    binary = "".join(bin)
    zerofix = (8 - len(binary)) * '0'
    return zerofix + binary

class SavePickle(object):
    r"""
    """

    def __init__(self, basedir, filename='pickle'):
        r"""SUMMARY

        __init__(basedir)

        @Arguments:
        - `basedir`:

        @Return:
        """
        self.basedir = basedir
        self._pickle_fname = filename

    @property
    def pickle_file(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        pickle_file()

        @Return:
        """
        return path.join(self.basedir, self._pickle_fname)

    def save_pickle(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        save()

        @Return:
        """
        with open(self.pickle_file, 'wb') as fobj:
            cPickle.dump(self, fobj, cPickle.HIGHEST_PROTOCOL)

    def resume(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        resume(basedir)

        @Arguments:
        - `basedir`:

        @Return:
        """
        return cPickle.load(
            open(path.join(self.basedir, self._pickle_fname), 'rb'))

class SavePickle(object):
    r"""
    """

    def __init__(self, filepath):
        r"""SUMMARY

        __init__(basedir)

        @Arguments:
        - `basedir`:

        @Return:
        """
        self.pickle_file = filepath

    def save_pickle(self, ):
        r"""SUMMARY

        save()

        @Return:
        """
        with open(self.pickle_file, 'wb') as fobj:
            cPickle.dump(self, fobj, cPickle.HIGHEST_PROTOCOL)


def pickle_resume(filepath):
    return cPickle.load(open(filepath, 'rb'))

    """
